//--------------------------------------------------------------
// Script Contents:
//--------------------------------------------------------------
// - All normal Kafra Employees in Towns/Dungeons/Fields/miscellaneous
// - The Kafra Corporation Headquarters / Kafra Special Reserve Points Gift Exchange NPCs
// - The Al De Baran Super Novice Cart Rental / Turbo Track Kafra Employees
//--------------------------------------------------------------


//--------------------------------------------------------------
// Alberta Kafra Employees - [Tsuyuki]
//--------------------------------------------------------------

alberta.gat,28,229,0	script	Kafra Employee	116,{

	if (kf_1_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_100_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_1000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_100000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	}
	cutin "kafra_02",2;
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "Welcome to the";
	mes "Kafra Corporation.";
	mes "Kafra's Employees are";
	mes "always ready to serve you.";
	mes "How can I help you today?";
	next;
	switch(select("Save","Use Storage","Use Teleport Service","Rent a Pushcart","Check Other Information","Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		savepoint "alberta.gat",31,231;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Respawn Point";
		mes "has been saved in the";
		mes "city of Alberta. Thank you";
		mes "for using the Kafra Service.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_02",255;
		end;
	case 2:
		if (getskilllv(1) < 6) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you";
			mes "need the Novice's";
			mes "Basic Skill Level 6 to";
			mes "use the Storage Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 50)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+5;
				set Zeny,Zeny-50;
			}
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Here, let me open";
			mes "your Storage for you.";
			mes "Thank you for using";
			mes "the Kafra Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			openstorage;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
			mes "have enough zeny to use";
			mes "the Storage Service. Our";
			mes "Storage access fee is 50 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Please choose";
		mes "your destination.";
		next;
		switch(select("Payon -> 1200 z","Morroc -> 1800 z","Prontera -> 1800z","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_02",255;
				warp "payon.gat",161,58;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Payon is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_02",255;
				end;
			}
		case 2:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1800)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1800;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
				}
				cutin "kafra_02",255;
				warp "morocc.gat",156,46;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Morroc is 1,800 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_02",255;
				end;
			}
		case 3:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1800)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1800;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
				}
				cutin "kafra_02",255;
				warp "prontera.gat",116,72;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Prontera is 1,800 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_02",255;
				end;
			}
		case 4:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths,";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_02",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 850 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart.","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 850) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
						set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+5;
						set Zeny,Zeny-850;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 850 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_02",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 5:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve Points.","Kafra Employee Locations","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			viewpoint 1,28,229,1,0x0000FF;
			viewpoint 1,113,60,2,0x0000FF;
			viewpoint 1,28,229,1,0x0000FF;
			viewpoint 1,113,60,2,0x0000FF;
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		case 3:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		}
	case 6:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_02",255;
		end;
	}
}

alb2trea.gat,59,69,5	script	Kafra Employee	117,{

	if (kf_1_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_100_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_1000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_100000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	}
	cutin "kafra_01",2;
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "Welcome to the";
	mes "Kafra Corporartion.";
	mes "The Kafra services";
	mes "are always on your side.";
	mes "How may I assist you?";
	next;
	switch(select("Use Storage","Check Other Information","Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		if (getskilllv(1) < 6) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you";
			mes "need the Novice's";
			mes "Basic Skill Level 6 to";
			mes "use the Storage Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 150)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+1;
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+5;
				set Zeny,Zeny-150;
			}
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Here, let me open";
			mes "your Storage for you.";
			mes "Thank you for using";
			mes "the Kafra Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			openstorage;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
			mes "have enough zeny to use";
			mes "the Storage Service. Our";
			mes "Storage access fee is 150 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		}
	case 2:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve Points.","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_01",255;
		end;
	}
}

aldeba_in.gat,84,166,4	script	Kafra Service	117,{

	cutin "kafra_01",2;
	mes "[Kafra Pavianne]";
	mes "Welcome! I'm Pavianne,";
	mes "one of the senior Kafra Employees. The Kafra Corporation Service is always trying to satisfy 100 % of our customers' expectations.";
	next;
	mes "[Kafra Pavianne]";
	mes "Due to a change in customer support policy, we no longer accept Kafra Passes. However, we are offering refunds for our customers who still possess these passes.";
	next;
	switch(select("Sell Kafra Pass","Alright, bye~")) {
	case 1:
		if (countitem(1084) == 0) {
			mes "[Kafra Pavianne]";
			mes "I'm sorry,";
			mes "but you don't";
			mes "have any Kafra Passes.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		} else {
			set '@kafrapass,countitem(1084);
			set '@passmoney,'@kafrapass * 2000;
			mes "[Kafra Pavianne]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			if ('@kafrapass == 1) {
				mes "You have 1 Kafra Pass.";
				mes "You can sell that pass to us for 2000 zeny. You you like to sell this Kafra Pass back to the Kafra Corporation?";
			} else {
				mes "You have "+'@kafrapass +", Kafra Passes.";
				mes "If you want to sell them to us, you will receive "+ passmoney +",zeny. Would you like to sell these back to the Kafra Corporation?";
			}
			next;
			switch(select("Yes","No")) {
			case 1:
				set '@kafrapass,countitem(1084);
				if ('@kafra_pass == 0) {
					mes "[Kafra Pavianne]";
					mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have any Kafra Passes.";
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_01",255;
					end;
				} else {
					delitem 1084,'@kafrapass;
					set Zeny,Zeny+'@passmoney;
					mes "[Kafra Pavianne]";
					mes "Thank you.";
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_01",255;
					end;
				}
				break;
			case 2:
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				end;
			}
		}
	case 2:
		mes "[Kafra Pavianne]";
		mes "Thank you,";
		mes "have a good day.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_01",255;
		end;
	}
}

aldeba_in.gat,79,161,7	script	Kafra Employee	115,{

	set '@max_max_c,checkweight(1201,1);
	if ('@max_max_c == 0) {
		mes "^3355FFWait a minute! Right now,";
		mes "you're carrying too many items";
		mes "in your inventory. Please come";
		mes "back after storing some of";
		mes "your things in Kafra Storage.";
		close;
	}
	while(1) {
		if (kf_100000_pit >= 10) {
			set kf_1000000_pit,kf_1000000_pit+1;
			set kf_100000_pit,kf_100000_pit-10;
		} else if (kf_10000_pit >= 10) {
			set kf_100000_pit,kf_100000_pit+1;
			set kf_10000_pit,kf_10000_pit-10;
		} else if (kf_1000_pit >= 10) {
			set kf_10000_pit,kf_10000_pit+1;
			set kf_1000_pit,kf_1000_pit-10;
		} else if (kf_100_pit >= 10) {
			set kf_1000_pit,kf_1000_pit+1;
			set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit-10;
		} else if (kf_10_pit >= 10) {
			set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
			set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit-10;
		} else if (kf_1_pit >= 10) {
			set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+1;
			set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit-10;
		} else {
			break;
		}
	}
	set '@now_weight,MaxWeight - Weight;
	set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
	set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
	set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
	set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
	set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
	set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
	set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "Welcome "+strcharinfo(0)+"~";
	mes "Here, you can exchange";
	mes "the Special Reserve Points";
	mes "you've earned by using the";
	mes "Kafra Services for some";
	mes "neat and useful prizes~";
	next;
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "Please remember that each window has a different amount of special reserve points you can Use";
	mes "You can use ^7D0781from 100p to 3000p^000000 in here.";
	next;
	if ('@now_weight < 11000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Um, but I don't think";
		mes "you're able to carry";
		mes "very much right now.";
		mes "It looks like you have";
		mes "too much stuff inside";
		mes "your inventory.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Please put some of";
		mes "your things into Kafra";
		mes "Storage. To use this";
		mes "service, we ask that you";
		mes "have about ^FF00001,100^000000 free units";
		mes "of weight in your inventory.";
		close;
	}
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "Let's see...";
	mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
	mes "Ah, you have a total of";
	mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
	mes "Now what you would like";
	mes "to exchange them for?";

aldebaran.gat,143,119,4	script	Kafra Employee	113,{

	if (kf_1_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_100_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_1000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_100000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	}
	cutin "kafra_05",2;
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "The Kafra Corporation";
	mes "is always working to provide";
	mes "you with convenient services.";
	mes "How may I be of assistance?";
	next;
	switch(select("Save","Use Storage","Use Teleport Service","Rent a Pushcart","Check Other Information","Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		savepoint "aldebaran.gat",168,112;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Respawn Point has";
		mes "been saved in the city of";
		mes "Al De Baran. Thank you";
		mes "for using the Kafra Service.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_05",255;
		end;
	case 2:
		if (getskilllv(1) < 6) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you";
			mes "need the Novice's";
			mes "Basic Skill Level 6 to";
			mes "use the Storage Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 20)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+2;
				set Zeny,Zeny-20;
			}
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Here, let me open";
			mes "your Storage for you.";
			mes "Thank you for using";
			mes "the Kafra Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			openstorage;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
			mes "have enough zeny to use";
			mes "the Storage Service. Our";
			mes "Storage access fee is 20 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Please choose";
		mes "your destination.";
		next;
		switch(select("Geffen -> 1200 z","Juno -> 1200 z","Izlude -> 1800 z","Mjolnir Dead Pit -> 1700z","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				warp "geffen.gat",120,39;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Geffen is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				end;
			}
		case 2:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				warp "yuno.gat",158,125;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Juno is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				end;
			}
		case 3:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1800)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1800;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
				}
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				warp "izlude.gat",94,103;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Izlude is 1,800 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				end;
			}
		case 4:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1700)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1700;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+7;
				}
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				warp "mjolnir_02.gat",99,351;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport to";
				mes "the Mjolnir Dead Pit is 1,700 zeny. ^FFFFFFcobo^000000";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				end;
			}
		case 5:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths,";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 600 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart.","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 600) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+6;
						set Zeny,Zeny-600;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_05",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 600 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_05",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_05",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 5:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve Points.","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		}
	case 6:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_05",255;
		end;
	}
}

aldebaran.gat,54,238,5	script	Kafra Employee	117,{

	if (Class == Job_Super_Novice) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		if (Sex == Male) {
			mes "Hello, Mister Super Novice~";
		} else {
			mes "Hello, Super Novice, Ma'am.";
		}
		mes "You must have been really";
		mes "dissapointed that the other";
		mes "Kafra Employees wouldn't let";
		mes "you rent a cart from them.";
		mes "But don't you worry now...";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "I'm here to support you guys";
		mes "by providing carts...";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "^3355FF*whispers*^000000";
		mes "^555555I am not supposed to do this";
		mes "because it's against our";
		mes "company policy. But I felt";
		mes "really sorry for Super Novices";
		mes "...so here I am.^000000";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Anyway, would you like to rent a cart? The service fee is 1,900 zeny.";
		next;
		switch(select("Rent a Cart.","Cancel.")) {
		case 1:
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Oh, here's the thing...";
			mes "Have you learned the 'Push Cart'";
			mes "skill? I can just rent you a";
			mes "cart, but if you haven't";
			mes "learned to push it, you'll";
			mes "just be wasting your zeny.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "So make sure that you have";
			mes "the 'Push Cart' skill already.";
			next;
			switch(select("Rent a Cart.","Cancel.")) {
			case 1:
				if (Cart) {
					mes "[Kafra Employee]";
					mes "Oh, you've already equipped a cart.";
					close;
				}
				if (Zeny > 1899) {
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+9;
					set Zeny,Zeny-1900;
					setcart;
					mes "[Kafra Employee]";
					mes "Thank you for using my service.";
					mes "Although what I am doing might";
					mes "not be legitimate to other";
					mes "Kafra Employees, I strongly";
					mes "believe I am doing what's right for the customers.";
					close;
				} else {
					mes "[Kafra Employee]";
					mes "I am sorry, but you do not have enough zeny with you. The service fee is 1,900 zeny.";
					close;
				}
			case 2:
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "Please come again.";
				mes "Thank you for using my services.";
				close;
		}
		case 2:
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Please come again.";
			mes "Thank you for using my services.";
			close;
		}
	} else {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Good da--Oops...!";
		mes "I don't think I can provide you";
		mes "with the services you want...";
		mes "Please go talk to another";
		mes "Kafra employee. I apologize";
		mes "for such inconvenience...";
		close;
	}
}

		cutin "kafra_03",255;
		end;
	case 2:
		if (getskilllv(1) < 6) {
			mes "[Kafra Staff]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you";
			mes "need the Novice's";
			mes "Basic Skill Level 6 to";
			mes "use the Storage Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 40)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+1;
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+5;
				set Zeny,Zeny-40;
			}
			mes "[Kafra Staff]";
			mes "Here, let me open";
			mes "your Storage for you.";
			mes "Thank you for using";
			mes "the Kafra Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			openstorage;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Staff]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
			mes "have enough zeny to use";
			mes "the Storage Service. Our";
			mes "Storage access fee is 40 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
		set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
		set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
		set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
		set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
		set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
		set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
		mes "[Kafra Staff]";
		mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+" has";
		mes ""+'@p_cal+" Special Reserve Points.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Staff]";
		mes "You can exchange";
		mes "Special Reserve Points";
		mes "for rewards in our main office";
		mes "in Al De Baran. Please use our";
		mes "convenient services to earn a";
		mes "chance to win some prizes~";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_03",255;
		end;
	case 4:
		mes "[Kafra Staff]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are trying our best to provide";
		mes "you with top quality service.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Staff]";
		mes "We are putting our greatest effort into providing our customers with services that are reliable and convenient through strict organization and management.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Staff]";
		mes "Thank you for using Kafra Corporation's services.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_03",255;
		end;
	}
}

	mes "How can I help you today?";
	next;
	switch(select("Save","Use Storage","Rent a Pushcart","Check Other Information","Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		savepoint "amatsu.gat",115,95;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Respawn Point";
		mes "has been saved here";
		mes "in the city of Amatsu.";

				delitem 7059,1;

			mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";

			mes "the Storage Service. Our";
			mes "Storage access fee is 80 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths,";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_02",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 700 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 700) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
						set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+5;
						set Zeny,Zeny-700;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 700 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_02",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 4:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+" 's special reserve is " + '@p_cal + ".";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;

			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 80)) {

				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {

			close2;
			cutin "kafra_07",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Please choose";
		mes "your destination.";
		next;
		switch(select(" Morroc -> 1200 z","Comodo -> 1200 z","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_07",255;

				end;
			} else {

				close2;
				cutin "kafra_07",255;
				end;
			}
		case 2:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_07",255;
				warp "comodo.gat",209,143;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Comodo is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_07",255;
				end;
			}
		case 3:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_07",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths,";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_07",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_07",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_07",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 1,000 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart.","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 1000) {
						set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
						set Zeny,Zeny-1000;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_07",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 1,000 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_07",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_07",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 5:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve Points.","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_07",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_07",255;
			end;
		}
	case 6:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_07",255;
		end;
	}
}

			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_08",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 850 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart.","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 850) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
						set Zeny,Zeny-850;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_08",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 850 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_08",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_08",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 5:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve Points.","Kafra Employee Locations","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			viewpoint 1,181,132,1,0x0000FF;
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		case 3:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		}
	case 6:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_08",255;
		end;
	}
}

	if (kf_1_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";

		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";

		close;
	} else if (kf_100_pit >= 25000) {

		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";

		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_1000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";

		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";

		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";

		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";

	}
	cutin "kafra_09",2;
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "Welcome to the";
	mes "Kafra Corporartion.";
	mes "The Kafra services";
	mes "are always on your side.";
	mes "How may I assist you?";
	next;
	switch(select("Save","Use Storage","Use Teleport Service","Rent a Pushcart","Check Other Information","Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Respawn Point has";
		mes "been saved in the city of";
		mes "Einbroch. Thank you for";
		mes "using the Kafra Service.";
		savepoint "einbroch.gat",239,198;
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_09",255;
		end;
	case 2:
		if (getskilllv(1) < 6) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you";
			mes "need the Novice's";
			mes "Basic Skill Level 6 to";
			mes "use the Storage Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 40)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set Zeny,Zeny-40;
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+4;
			}
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Here, let me open";
			mes "your Storage for you.";
			mes "Thank you for using";
			mes "the Kafra Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			openstorage;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
			mes "have enough zeny to use";
			mes "the Storage Service. Our";
			mes "Storage access fee is 40 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Because of the ^FF0000Limited";
		mes "Transport Agreement^000000, the";
		mes "Kafra Corporation cannot";
		mes "provide Teleport Services";
		mes "in the Schwaltzvalt Republic.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We ask that you please";
		mes "use the Airship Service";
		mes "instead. Thank you for your";
		mes "understanding and cooperation.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_09",255;
		end;
	case 4:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;

			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		} else {

				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_09",255;
				end;
			} else {

					}

					end;
				}

		}
	case 5:

	}
	cutin "kafra_03",2;
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "Welcome~!";
	mes "The Kafra Services";
	mes "are always on your side.";
	mes "So how can I help you?";
	next;
	switch(select("Save","Use Storage","Use Teleport Service","Rent a Pushcart","Check Other Information","Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		savepoint "geffen.gat",120,38;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";

		mes "city of Geffen. Thank you";
		mes "for using the Kafra Service.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_03",255;

			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 30)) {

				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+3;

			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;

		mes "Please choose your destination.";
		next;
		switch(select("Prontera -> 1200 z","Al De Baran -> 1200 z","Orc Dungeon -> 1700 z","Mjolnir Dead Pit -> 1700z","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;

				warp "prontera.gat",116,72;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Prontera is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_03",255;
				end;
			}
		case 2:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_03",255;
				warp "aldebaran.gat",168,112;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Al De Baran is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_03",255;
				end;
			}
		case 3:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1700)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1700;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+7;
				}
				cutin "kafra_03",255;
				warp "gef_fild10.gat",52,326;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport to";
				mes "the Orc Dungeon is 1,700 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_03",255;
				end;
			}
		case 4:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1700)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1700;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+7;
				}
				cutin "kafra_03",255;
				warp "mjolnir_02.gat",99,351;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport to";
				mes "the Mjolnir Dead Pit is 1,700 zeny. ^FFFFFFcobo^000000";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_03",255;
				end;
			}
		case 5:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths,";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_03",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 750 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart.","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 750) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+7;
						set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+5;
						set Zeny,Zeny-750;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_03",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 750 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_03",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_03",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 5:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve Points.","Kafra Employee Locations","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			viewpoint 1,120,62,1,0x0000FF;
			viewpoint 1,203,123,2,0x0000FF;
			viewpoint 1,120,62,1,0x0000FF;
			viewpoint 1,203,123,2,0x0000FF;
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;
		case 3:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_03",255;
			end;
		}
	case 6:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_03",255;
		end;
	}
}

		mes "your destination.";
		next;
		switch(select("Al De Baran -> 1200z","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_08",255;
				warp "aldebaran.gat",168,112;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Al De Baran is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_08",255;
				end;
			}
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths,";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_08",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 800 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart.","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 800) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
						set Zeny,Zeny-800;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_08",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 800 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_08",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_08",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 5:
		switch(select("Special Reserve","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		}
	case 6:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_08",255;
		end;
	}
}

		cutin "kafra_09",255;
		end;
	case 2:

			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you";
			mes "need the Novice's";
			mes "Basic Skill Level 6 to";
			mes "use the Storage Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 40)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+4;
				set Zeny,Zeny-40;
			}
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Here, let me open";

	case 2:
		if (getskilllv(1) < 6) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you";
			mes "need the Novice's";
			mes "Basic Skill Level 6 to";
			mes "use the Storage Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 50)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+5;
				set Zeny,Zeny-80;
			}
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Here, let me open";
			mes "your Storage for you.";
			mes "Thank you for using";
			mes "the Kafra Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			openstorage;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
			mes "have enough zeny to use";
			mes "the Storage Service. Our";
			mes "Storage access fee is 80 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths,";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_02",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 700 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 700) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
						set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+5;
						set Zeny,Zeny-700;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 700 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_02",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_02",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 4:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+" 's special reserve is " + '@p_cal + ".";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_02",255;
			end;
		}
	case 5:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_02",255;
		end;
	}
}

lighthalzen.gat,164,100,4	script	Kafra Employee	860,{

	if (kf_1_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";

		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";

	}
	cutin "kafra_08",2;
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "Welcome to the";
	mes "Kafra Corporartion.";
	mes "The Kafra services";
	mes "are always on your side.";
	mes "How may I assist you?";
	next;
	switch(select("Save","Use Storage","Use Teleport Service","Rent a Pushcart","Check Other Information","Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		savepoint "lighthalzen.gat",159,95;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Respawn Point has";
		mes "been saved in Lighthalzen.";
		mes "Thank you for continuing";
		mes "to use the Kafra Service.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_08",255;
		end;
	case 2:
		if (getskilllv(1) < 6) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";

			close2;
			cutin "kafra_08",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 40)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;

		mes "Kafra Corporation cannot";
		mes "provide Teleport Services";
		mes "in the Schwaltzvalt Republic.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We ask that you please";
		mes "use the Airship Service";
		mes "instead. Thank you for your";
		mes "understanding and cooperation.";
		close2;

			mes "Storage access fee is 40 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Because of the ^FF0000Limited";
		mes "Transport Agreement^000000, the";
		mes "Kafra Corporation cannot";
		mes "provide Teleport Services";
		mes "in the Schwaltzvalt Republic.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We ask that you please";
		mes "use the Airship Service";
		mes "instead. Thank you for your";
		mes "understanding and cooperation.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_09",255;
		end;
	case 4:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths,";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_09",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 800 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart.","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 800) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
						set Zeny,Zeny-800;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_09",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 800 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_09",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_09",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 5:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve Points.","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_09",255;
			end;
		}
	case 6:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_09",255;
		end;
	}
}

			end;

		savepoint "morocc.gat",190,283;

				delitem 7059,1;

		next;
		switch(select("Prontera -> 1200 z","Payon -> 1200 z","Alberta -> 1800 z","Comodo -> 1800 z","Paros Lighthouse -> 1200z","Cancel")) {

					delitem 7060,1;

				warp "prontera.gat",116,72;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";

				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Prontera is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_04",255;
				end;
			}
		case 2:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_04",255;
				warp "payon.gat",161,58;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Payon is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_04",255;
				end;
			}
		case 3:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1800)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1800;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
				}
				cutin "kafra_04",255;
				warp "alberta.gat",117,56;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";

				close2;
				cutin "kafra_04",255;

			mes "use the Storage Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 60)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+6;
				set Zeny,Zeny-60;
			}
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Here, let me open";

			openstorage;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
			mes "have enough zeny to use";
			mes "the Storage Service. Our";
			mes "Storage access fee is 60 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Please choose";
		mes "your destination.";
		next;
		switch(select("Prontera -> 1200 z","Alberta -> 1200 z","Morroc -> 1200 z","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				warp "prontera.gat",116,72;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Prontera is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				end;
			}
		case 2:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				warp "alberta.gat",117,56;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Alberta is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				end;
			}
		case 3:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				warp "morocc.gat",156,46;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Morroc is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				end;
			}
		case 4:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Master Smiths,";
			mes "Alchemists and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_05",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 930 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart.","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 930) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+9;
						set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+3;
						set Zeny,Zeny-930;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_05",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 930 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_05",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_05",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 5:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve Points.","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_05",255;
			end;
		}
	case 6:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_05",255;
		end;
	}
}

			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_01",255;
		end;
	}

prontera.gat,146,89,6	script	Kafra Employee	117,{

	if (kf_1_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_100_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_1000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	} else if (kf_10000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";

		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";

		close;
	} else if (kf_100000_pit >= 25000) {
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Special Reserve Points";
		mes "have exceeded the maximum";
		mes "capacity. Please redeem these";
		mes "points at the Kafra Corportation Headquarters in Al De Baran";
		mes "before using the Kafra Service.";
		close;
	}
	cutin "kafra_01",2;
	mes "[Kafra Employee]";
	mes "Welcome to the";
	mes "Kafra Corporartion.";
	mes "The Kafra services";
	mes "are always on your side.";
	mes "How may I assist you?";
	next;
	switch(select("Save","Use Storage","Use Teleport Service","Rent a Pushcart","Check Other Information","Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		savepoint "prontera.gat",116,72;
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Your Respawn Point has";
		mes "been saved in the city of";
		mes "Prontera. Thank you for";
		mes "using the Kafra Service.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_01",255;
		end;
	case 2:
		if (getskilllv(1) < 6) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you";
			mes "need the Novice's";
			mes "Basic Skill Level 6 to";
			mes "use the Storage Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		} else if ((countitem(7059) != 0) || (Zeny >= 40)) {
			if (countitem(7059) != 0) {
				delitem 7059,1;
			} else {
				set Zeny,Zeny-40;
				set kf_1_pit,kf_1_pit+4;
			}
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Here, let me open";
			mes "your Storage for you.";
			mes "Thank you for using";
			mes "the Kafra Service.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			openstorage;
			end;
		} else {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but you don't";
			mes "have enough zeny to use";
			mes "the Storage Service. Our";
			mes "Storage access fee is 40 zeny.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		}
	case 3:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "Please choose";
		mes "your destination.";
		next;
		switch(select("Izlude -> 600 z","Geffen -> 1200 z","Payon -> 1200 z","Morroc -> 1200 z","Orc Dungeon -> 1700 z","Alberta -> 1800z","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 600)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-600;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+6;
				}
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				warp "izlude.gat",91,105;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Izlude is 600 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				end;
			}
		case 2:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				warp "geffen.gat",120,39;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Geffen is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				end;
			}
		case 3:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				warp "payon.gat",161,58;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Payon is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				end;
			}
		case 4:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1200)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1200;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+2;
				}
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				warp "morocc.gat",156,46;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport";
				mes "to Morroc is 1,200 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				end;
			}
		case 5:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1700)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1700;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+7;
				}
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				warp "gef_fild10.gat",52,326;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";
				mes "Service. The fee to teleport to";
				mes "the Orc Dungeon is 1,700 zeny.";
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				end;
			}
		case 6:
			if ((countitem(7060) != 0) || (Zeny >= 1800)) {
				if (countitem(7060) != 0) {
					delitem 7060,1;
				} else {
					set Zeny,Zeny-1800;
					set kf_100_pit,kf_100_pit+1;
					set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
				}
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				warp "alberta.gat",117,56;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "I'm sorry, but you don't have";
				mes "enough zeny for the Teleport";

		case 7:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		}
	case 4:
		if ((Class != Job_Merchant) && (Class != Job_Blacksmith) && (Class != Job_Alchemist)) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but the";
			mes "Pushcart rental service";
			mes "is only available to Merchants,";
			mes "Blacksmiths, Alchemists, Master";
			mes "Smiths and Biochemists.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		} else if (Cart) {
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You already have";
			mes "a Pushcart equipped.";
			mes "Unfortunately, we can't";
			mes "rent more than one to";
			mes "each customer at a time.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		} else {
			if (countitem(7061) != 0) {
				delitem 7061,1;
				setcart;
				close2;
				cutin "kafra_01",255;
				end;
			} else {
				mes "[Kafra Employee]";
				mes "The Pushcart rental";
				mes "fee is 800 zeny. Would";
				mes "you like to rent a Pushcart?";
				next;
				switch(select("Rent a Pushcart.","Cancel")) {
				case 1:
					if (Zeny >= 800) {
						set kf_10_pit,kf_10_pit+8;
						set Zeny,Zeny-800;
						setcart;
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_01",255;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Employee]";
						mes "I'm sorry, but you";
						mes "don't have enough";
						mes "zeny to pay the Pushcart";
						mes "rental fee of 800 zeny.";
						close2;
						cutin "kafra_01",255;
						end;
					}
				case 2:
					close2;
					cutin "kafra_01",255;
					end;
				}
			}
		}
	case 5:
		switch(select("Check Special Reserve Points.","Kafra Employee Locations","Cancel")) {
		case 1:
			set '@p_10_cal,kf_1_pit * 1;
			set '@p_100_cal,kf_10_pit * 10;
			set '@p_1000_cal,kf_100_pit * 100;
			set '@p_10000_cal,kf_1000_pit * 1000;
			set '@p_100000_cal,kf_10000_pit * 10000;
			set '@p_1000000_cal,kf_100000_pit * 100000;
			set '@p_cal,'@p_10_cal + '@p_100_cal + '@p_1000_cal + '@p_10000_cal + '@p_100000_cal + '@p_1000000_cal;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "Let's see...";
			mes ""+strcharinfo(0)+"...";
			mes "Ah, you have a total of";
			mes ""+ '@p_cal + " Special Reserve Points.";
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Employee]";
			mes "You can exchange your";
			mes "Special Reserve Points for";
			mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Al De Baran. Please use our";
			mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		case 2:
			viewpoint 1,146,89,1,0x0000FF;
			viewpoint 1,282,200,2,0x0000FF;
			viewpoint 1,151,29,3,0x0000FF;
			viewpoint 1,29,207,4,0x0000FF;
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		case 3:
			close2;
			cutin "kafra_01",255;
			end;
		}
	case 6:
		mes "[Kafra Employee]";
		mes "We, here at Kafra Corporation,";
		mes "are always endeavoring to provide you with the best services. We hope that we meet your adventuring needs and standards of excellence.";
		close2;
		cutin "kafra_01",255;
		end;
	}
}
